<p><b>Lauren Ann Williams</b><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-2"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NotLikeaBitch_7-0"><a href="#cite_note-NotLikeaBitch-7">[7]</a></sup> (born September 13, 1981)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SLAM_1-4"><a href="#cite_note-SLAM-1">[1]</a></sup> is a <a href="/wiki/Canadians" title="Canadians">Canadian</a> <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling" title="Professional wrestling">professional wrestler</a> currently signed to <a href="/wiki/Total_Nonstop_Action_Wrestling" title="Total Nonstop Action Wrestling">Total Nonstop Action Wrestling</a> (TNA) under the <a href="/wiki/Ring_name" title="Ring name">ring name</a> <b>Angelina Love</b>. In TNA, she has held the <a href="/wiki/TNA_Knockouts_Championship" title="TNA Knockouts Championship">Knockouts Championship</a> a record-tying six times (along with <a href="/wiki/Gail_Kim" title="Gail Kim">Gail Kim</a>), and was a one-time <a href="/wiki/TNA_Knockouts_Tag_Team_Championship" title="TNA Knockouts Tag Team Championship">Knockouts Tag Team Champion</a> with <a href="/wiki/Katarina_Waters" title="Katarina Waters">Winter</a>. Outside of TNA, she works under the ring name <b>Angel Williams</b>.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Professional_wrestling_career">Professional wrestling career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Professional wrestling career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Williams debuted in wrestling in 2000, working for <a href="/wiki/Independent_circuit" title="Independent circuit">independent promotions</a> around Canada under the ring name Angel Williams. Her all-time favorite wrestler <a href="/wiki/Shawn_Michaels" title="Shawn Michaels">Shawn Michaels</a> was her inspiration to get into wrestling. She was first a <a href="/wiki/Manager_(professional_wrestling)" title="Manager (professional wrestling)">valet</a> for various wrestlers such as <a href="/wiki/Chris_Sabin" title="Chris Sabin">Chris Sabin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Eric_Young_(wrestler)" title="Eric Young (wrestler)">Eric Young</a>, and then began in-ring training under Rob Fuego.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SLAM_1-5"><a href="#cite_note-SLAM-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Total_Nonstop_Action_Wrestling_.282004.29">Total Nonstop Action Wrestling (2004)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Total Nonstop Action Wrestling (2004)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Williams briefly worked for <a href="/wiki/Total_Nonstop_Action_Wrestling" title="Total Nonstop Action Wrestling">Total Nonstop Action Wrestling</a> (TNA) in 2004, mainly wrestling on <i><a href="/wiki/TNA_Xplosion" title="TNA Xplosion">TNA Xplosion</a></i> against <a href="/wiki/Trinity_(wrestler)" title="Trinity (wrestler)">Trinity</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WWE_deal_8-0"><a href="#cite_note-WWE_deal-8">[8]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Wrestling_Entertainment">World Wrestling Entertainment</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: World Wrestling Entertainment">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Deep_South_Wrestling_.282004.E2.80.932007.29">Deep South Wrestling (2004–2007)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Deep South Wrestling (2004–2007)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Williams was working for promotions in the United States when <a href="/wiki/WWE" title="WWE">World Wrestling Entertainment</a> (WWE) scouted her, and invited her to a tryout in June 2004.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WWE_deal_8-1"><a href="#cite_note-WWE_deal-8">[8]</a></sup> In November, she trained at WWE's then-<a href="/wiki/Farm_team" title="Farm team">developmental territory</a> <a href="/wiki/Ohio_Valley_Wrestling" title="Ohio Valley Wrestling">Ohio Valley Wrestling</a> (OVW), and WWE signed her to a contract in late 2004.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-3"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WWE_deal_8-2"><a href="#cite_note-WWE_deal-8">[8]</a></sup> She was assigned to wrestle and train in another WWE developmental territory, <a href="/wiki/Deep_South_Wrestling" title="Deep South Wrestling">Deep South Wrestling</a> (DSW). Williams began managing <a href="/wiki/Johnny_Swinger" title="Johnny Swinger">Johnny Parisi</a> in the summer of 2005.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-4"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> On the September 8, 2005 episode of <i>DSW TV</i>, Williams made her in-ring debut by defeating <a href="/wiki/Michelle_McCool" title="Michelle McCool">Michelle McCool</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-5"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> On September 22, Williams was scheduled to wrestle against McCool, but MCcool never showed up.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-6"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> Instead Daisy Mae came out, challenged Williams and Williams defeated Mae in a singles match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-7"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> At the February 9, 2006 episode of <i>DSW TV</i>, Williams participated in the first ever Bikini Contest in DSW. She did not reveal her bikini because <a href="/wiki/Brian_Mailhot" title="Brian Mailhot">Palmer Cannon</a> interrupted, which led to a match, where Love managed Cannon against <a href="/wiki/Tommy_Dreamer" title="Tommy Dreamer">Tommy Dreamer</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-8"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> On February 28, she underwent knee surgery in <a href="/wiki/Birmingham,_Alabama" title="Birmingham, Alabama">Birmingham, Alabama</a> to repair a <a href="/wiki/Anterior_cruciate_ligament_injury" title="Anterior cruciate ligament injury">torn ACL</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SLAMBio_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-SLAMBio-9">[9]</a></sup> After almost seven months of rehab, she stepped back into the ring at a DSW TV taping.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-9"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> At the beginning of November 2006, Williams started managing <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shane_Twins" title="Shane Twins">The Gymini</a>, but The Gymini were released from their contracts in January 2007.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-10"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<p>Williams then began a feud with <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_authority_figures" title="Professional wrestling authority figures">General Manager</a> of DSW, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kristin_Eubanks" title="Kristin Eubanks">Krissy Vaine</a>, with Williams claiming that Vaine did something immoral to be appointed General Manager. Over the next couple of weeks, Vaine would cost Williams her matches by forcing other DSW Divas into interfering in Williams's matches.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-11"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> On the January 4 episode of <i>DSW TV</i>, Williams defeated the debuting <a href="/wiki/Brooke_Tessmacher" title="Brooke Tessmacher">Brooke Adams</a>, with Vaine on commentary.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-12"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> On the January 11 episode of <i>DSW TV'</i>, Williams competed against <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shantelle_Taylor" title="Shantelle Taylor">Shantelle Taylor</a> in a losing effort.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-13"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> On the January 18 episode of <i>DSW TV</i>, Williams teamed up with Shantelle in a winning effort, defeating Luscious and Tracy Taylor in a tag-team match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-14"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> On the February 8 episode of <i>DSW TV</i>, Williams defeated Krissy Vaine by disqualification after <a href="/wiki/Melissa_Coates" title="Melissa Coates">The Bag Lady</a> attacked Williams. Immediately following the match, Vaine ordered the match to restart, resulting in Vaine pinning Williams.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-15"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> The following week, Williams got a measure of revenge by defeating The Bag Lady.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-16"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> On the April 5, 2007 episode of <i>DSW TV</i>, Williams accompanied Vaine to a match, where she defeated <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Natalya_(wrestler)" title="Natalya (wrestler)">Nattie Neidhart</a> after interference from Williams.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-17"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> Over the following weeks, Williams teamed up with Vaine against Neidhart and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shantelle_Malawski" title="Shantelle Malawski">Shantelle Taylor</a>, losing to them on several occasions.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-18"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> The storyline, however, came to an end when Deep South Wrestling shut down in April.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-19"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ohio_Valley_Wrestling_.282007.29">Ohio Valley Wrestling (2007)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Ohio Valley Wrestling (2007)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After DSW shut down, Williams was moved to Ohio Valley Wrestling. Williams made her OVW debut in a <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_professional_wrestling_terms#D" title="Glossary of professional wrestling terms">dark match</a> at the May 16, 2007 television tapings in <a href="/wiki/Louisville,_Kentucky" title="Louisville, Kentucky">Louisville, Kentucky</a>, defeating <a href="/wiki/Serena_Deeb" title="Serena Deeb">Serena</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup> Two days later, Williams was released from her developmental contract.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-20"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Independent_circuit_.282007.E2.80.932014.29">Independent circuit (2007–2014)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Independent circuit (2007–2014)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>After being released from WWE, Williams resurfaced in Mexican promotion <a href="/wiki/Asistencia_Asesor%C3%ADa_y_Administraci%C3%B3n" title="Asistencia Asesoría y Administración">Asistencia Asesoría y Administración</a> (AAA), under the name Canadian Angel on June 10, 2007.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup> She also appeared for other independent promotions such as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NWA:_Extreme_Canadian_Championship_Wrestling" title="NWA: Extreme Canadian Championship Wrestling">NWA: Extreme Canadian Championship Wrestling</a> and Full Throttle Wrestling.</p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Angelina2011.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="637" data-file-width="498" height="217" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Angelina2011.png/170px-Angelina2011.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Angelina2011.png/255px-Angelina2011.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Angelina2011.png/340px-Angelina2011.png 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Angelina2011.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Love in July 2011</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Love made her debut for Great Canadian Wrestling (GCW) on December 27, 2011 at the <i>Season's Beatings</i> event in <a href="/wiki/Oshawa" title="Oshawa">Oshawa, Ontario, Canada</a>, where she teamed up with <a href="/wiki/Tye_Dillinger" title="Tye Dillinger">Shawn Spears</a> in a losing effort to Seleziya Sparx and Brent Banks in a mixed-tag-team match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CAGEMATCHS_12-0"><a href="#cite_note-CAGEMATCHS-12">[12]</a></sup> Love made her debut for Indian promotion <a href="/wiki/Ring_Ka_King" title="Ring Ka King">Ring Ka King</a> on March 18, 2012, where she defeated <a href="/wiki/Cheerleader_Melissa" title="Cheerleader Melissa">Alissa Flash</a>. After the match, Love began a storyline in which she was being pursed by Romeo and Zoravar.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-21"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CAGEMATCHS_12-1"><a href="#cite_note-CAGEMATCHS-12">[12]</a></sup> On the April 4 episode of <i>Ring Ka King</i>, Love defeated Raisha and Alissa Flash in a triple-treat match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CAGEMATCHS_12-2"><a href="#cite_note-CAGEMATCHS-12">[12]</a></sup> Following the match, Romeo came to the ring with a gift for Love, but Zoravar would out-do Romeo by giving Love jewelry and a car.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-22"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> On the April 14 episode of <i>Ring Ka King</i>, Love defeated Raisha in a singles match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CAGEMATCHS_12-3"><a href="#cite_note-CAGEMATCHS-12">[12]</a></sup> Following the match, Zoravar confessed that he was in love with Love.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-23"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CAGEMATCHS_12-4"><a href="#cite_note-CAGEMATCHS-12">[12]</a></sup> On September 22, 2012, during her time with <a href="/wiki/Total_Nonstop_Action_Wrestling" title="Total Nonstop Action Wrestling">TNA</a>, Love and <a href="/wiki/Velvet_Sky" title="Velvet Sky">Velvet Sky</a> reunited as <a href="/wiki/The_Beautiful_People_(professional_wrestling)" title="The Beautiful People (professional wrestling)">The Beautiful People</a> at a Northeast Wrestling event, where they were defeated by <a href="/wiki/Madison_Rayne" title="Madison Rayne">Madison Rayne</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thea_Trinidad" title="Thea Trinidad">Rosita</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup></p>
<p>Love made her debut for <a href="/wiki/Family_Wrestling_Entertainment" title="Family Wrestling Entertainment">Family Wrestling Entertainment</a> (FWE) on October 4, 2012 at the <i>Back 2 Brooklyn</i> internet pay-per-view, where she teamed up with Velvet Sky to defeat the <a href="/wiki/FWE_Women%27s_Championship" title="FWE Women's Championship">FWE Women's Champion</a> <a href="/wiki/Maria_Kanellis" title="Maria Kanellis">Maria Kanellis</a> and <a href="/wiki/Katarina_Waters" title="Katarina Waters">Katrina Lea</a> a in a tag team match, with Love pinning Kanellis.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FWEDebut_15-0"><a href="#cite_note-FWEDebut-15">[15]</a></sup> Because of the win, Williams was named number one contender, and faced Kanellis for the FWE Women's Championship on February 16, 2013, but was unsuccessful in winning the championship after <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Michael_Bennett_(wrestler)" title="Michael Bennett (wrestler)">Mike Bennett</a> helped Maria take advantage.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FWENoLimits_16-0"><a href="#cite_note-FWENoLimits-16">[16]</a></sup> On November 10, Love made her debut for <a href="/wiki/Pro-Wrestling:_EVE" title="Pro-Wrestling: EVE">Pro-Wrestling: EVE</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sudbury,_Suffolk" title="Sudbury, Suffolk">Sudbury, Suffolk</a>, <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>, defeating Carmel Jacob by disqualification, following interference from Sara-Marie Taylor.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EVEWrestleFever_17-0"><a href="#cite_note-EVEWrestleFever-17">[17]</a></sup> Love then teamed with Erin Angel in a tag team match, where they were defeated by Jacob and Taylor.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EVEWrestleFever_17-1"><a href="#cite_note-EVEWrestleFever-17">[17]</a></sup> On February 16, 2013, at <i>FWE No Limits</i>, Love was defeated by the FWE Women's Champion Maria Kanellis in a title match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup> Love returned to FWE at their <i>Openweight Grand Prix</i> on October 12, defeating <a href="/wiki/Cheerleader_Melissa" title="Cheerleader Melissa">Cheerleader Melissa</a> and <a href="/wiki/Serena_Deeb" title="Serena Deeb">Serena Deeb</a> in a three-way match, when she pinned Deeb.</p>
<p>On February 22, 2013, <a href="/wiki/Daffney" title="Daffney">Daffney</a> announced that Love would be making her debut in the all-female promotion <a href="/wiki/Shine_Wrestling" title="Shine Wrestling">Shine Wrestling</a>, at the event <i>Shine 8</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup> At <i>Shine 8</i> on March 23, Love teamed up with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mia_Yim" title="Mia Yim">Mia Yim</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kia_Stevens" title="Kia Stevens">Amazing Kong</a> and <a href="/wiki/Christina_Von_Eerie" title="Christina Von Eerie">Christina Von Eerie</a> in a losing effort to the team of Valkyrie (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Allysin_Kay" title="Allysin Kay">Allysin Kay</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ivelisse_V%C3%A9lez" title="Ivelisse Vélez">Ivelisse</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bonnie_Maxon" title="Bonnie Maxon">Rain</a> and Taylor Made).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Shine8_20-0"><a href="#cite_note-Shine8-20">[20]</a></sup> On April 19, at the <i>Shine 9</i> event, Love competed in the <a href="/wiki/Shine_Championship" title="Shine Championship">Shine Championship</a> qualifying tournament, losing to Rain.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Shine9_21-0"><a href="#cite_note-Shine9-21">[21]</a></sup> On May 24 at the <i>Shine 10</i> event, Love was unsuccessful in winning the Shine Championship from the reigning champion Rain.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Shine10_22-0"><a href="#cite_note-Shine10-22">[22]</a></sup> Love returned on January 24 at the <i>Shine 14</i> event, where she defeated <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Leah_von_Dutch" title="Leah von Dutch">Leah von Dutch</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FinalSHINE_23-0"><a href="#cite_note-FinalSHINE-23">[23]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Asistencia_Asesor.C3.ADa_y_Administraci.C3.B3n_.282007.3B_2011.29">Asistencia Asesoría y Administración (2007; 2011)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Asistencia Asesoría y Administración (2007; 2011)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In June 2007 Williams made several appearances for Mexican promotion <a href="/wiki/Asistencia_Asesor%C3%ADa_y_Administraci%C3%B3n" title="Asistencia Asesoría y Administración">Asistencia Asesoría y Administración</a> (AAA) as a member of <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Foreign_Legion_(wrestling)" title="Foreign Legion (wrestling)">La Legión Extranjera</a></i> (Foreign Legion) under the ring name Canadian Angel.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-24"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<p>She returned to the promotion on June 18, 2011, at <a href="/wiki/Tripleman%C3%ADa_XIX" title="Triplemanía XIX">Triplemanía XIX</a>, where she teamed with <a href="/wiki/Mickie_James" title="Mickie James">Mickie James</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sexy_Star" title="Sexy Star">Sexy Star</a> and <a href="/wiki/Velvet_Sky" title="Velvet Sky">Velvet Sky</a> to defeat <a href="/wiki/Cynthia_Moreno" title="Cynthia Moreno">Cynthia Moreno</a>, <a href="/wiki/Faby_Apache" title="Faby Apache">Faby Apache</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mari_Apache" title="Mari Apache">Mari Apache</a> and Lolita in an eight-woman tag team match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_TNA">Return to TNA</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Return to TNA">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Beautiful_People_.282007.E2.80.932009.29">The Beautiful People (2007–2009)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: The Beautiful People (2007–2009)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/The_Beautiful_People_(professional_wrestling)" title="The Beautiful People (professional wrestling)">The Beautiful People</a></div>
<p>In September 2007, she was contacted again by TNA to appear at their annual pay-per-view <a href="/wiki/Bound_for_Glory_(2007)" title="Bound for Glory (2007)">Bound for Glory</a>, which was confirmed on the October 9 episode of <i><a href="/wiki/TNA_Today" title="TNA Today">TNA Today</a></i> where she was interviewed by <a href="/wiki/Jeremy_Borash" title="Jeremy Borash">Jeremy Borash</a>. At Bound For Glory, Williams participated in a 10 Knockout Gauntlet to crown the first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/TNA_Women%27s_Knockout_Championship" title="TNA Women's Knockout Championship">TNA Women's Champion</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BFG07_25-0"><a href="#cite_note-BFG07-25">[25]</a></sup> During the match, she was eliminated by <a href="/wiki/Gail_Kim" title="Gail Kim">Gail Kim</a> and <a href="/wiki/ODB_(wrestler)" title="ODB (wrestler)">ODB</a>, and the match was won in the end by Kim.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BFG07_25-1"><a href="#cite_note-BFG07-25">[25]</a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/TNA_Genesis#2007" title="TNA Genesis">Genesis</a> pay-per-view, Williams unsuccessfully challenged for the Knockouts Championship in a fatal-four way with Gail Kim retaining her title.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup></p>
<p>Williams soon began competing under the ring name <b>"Angelina Love"</b> and formed a partnership with <a href="/wiki/Velvet_Sky" title="Velvet Sky">Velvet Sky</a>, calling themselves "Velvet-Love Entertainment", later changed to "<a href="/wiki/The_Beautiful_People_(professional_wrestling)" title="The Beautiful People (professional wrestling)">The Beautiful People</a>". The duo defeated ODB and <a href="/wiki/Nicole_Raczynski" title="Nicole Raczynski">Roxxi Laveaux</a> at <a href="/wiki/TNA_Turning_Point#2007" title="TNA Turning Point">Turning Point</a> in a Knockouts Tag Team match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TurningPoint2007_3-1"><a href="#cite_note-TurningPoint2007-3">[3]</a></sup> During the following months, Love and Sky also aided Gail Kim in her rivalry with <a href="/wiki/Kia_Stevens" title="Kia Stevens">Awesome Kong</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TurningPoint2007_3-2"><a href="#cite_note-TurningPoint2007-3">[3]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup> Love and Sky became <a href="/wiki/Heel_(professional_wrestling)" title="Heel (professional wrestling)">villains</a> on the March 13, 2008, episode of <i>Impact</i> by attacking Laveaux.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-25"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup> Love also participated at <a href="/wiki/Lockdown_(2008)" title="Lockdown (2008)">Lockdown</a> in the first ever <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_match_types#Cages" title="Professional wrestling match types">"Queen of the Cage" match</a> but was pinned by Laveaux.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:The_Beautiful_People_TNA.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="360" height="227" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/The_Beautiful_People_TNA.jpg/170px-The_Beautiful_People_TNA.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/The_Beautiful_People_TNA.jpg/255px-The_Beautiful_People_TNA.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/The_Beautiful_People_TNA.jpg/340px-The_Beautiful_People_TNA.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:The_Beautiful_People_TNA.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/The_Beautiful_People_(professional_wrestling)" title="The Beautiful People (professional wrestling)">The Beautiful People</a> (Love and <a href="/wiki/Velvet_Sky" title="Velvet Sky">Velvet Sky</a>) with <a href="/wiki/Billy_Gunn" title="Billy Gunn">Cute Kip</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Adopting the personas of superficial <a href="/wiki/Prima_donna" title="Prima donna">prima donnas</a>, who loathe and insult anyone they consider to be <a href="/wiki/Physical_attractiveness" title="Physical attractiveness">physically unattractive</a>, they dropped the Velvet-Love Entertainment moniker and became The Beautiful People. In 2008 at <a href="/wiki/Lockdown_(2008)" title="Lockdown (2008)">Lockdown</a>, they participated in the first ever "<a href="/wiki/TNA_Knockout#Queen_of_the_Cage" title="TNA Knockout">Queen of the Cage</a>" match, which was won by Roxxi, when she defeated Love in the finals.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pwlock08_29-0"><a href="#cite_note-pwlock08-29">[29]</a></sup> The following month's pay-per-view, <a href="/wiki/TNA_Sacrifice#2008" title="TNA Sacrifice">Sacrifice</a>, saw a <a href="/wiki/Battle_royal_(professional_wrestling)" title="Battle royal (professional wrestling)">Battle Royal</a> where the last two in the ring competed in a <a href="/wiki/Ladder_match" title="Ladder match">Ladder match</a> with the loser having their head shaved; the week before on <i>Impact!</i> Gail Kim won immunity in a Shears-On-A-Pole-Match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp0905_30-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp0905-30">[30]</a></sup> The Makeover Battle Royal-Ladder Match saw Kim and Roxxi survive the Battle Royal and with Kim having immunity this meant the third runner-up, Angelina Love, would have her head shaved if Roxxi won. Knowing this, Love interfered in the Ladder Match to ensure Kim's victory and Roxxi's head being shaved bald. While the Knockouts watched the haircut in pity, Love and Sky paraded around celebrating with Roxxi's freshly shaved hair cementing them as villains in one of TNA's most controversial moments.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sacr08_31-0"><a href="#cite_note-sacr08-31">[31]</a></sup></p>
<p>The Beautiful People continued to harass the fan favorite Knockouts, including ruining Kim's chance at winning the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/TNA_Women%27s_Knockout_Championship" title="TNA Women's Knockout Championship">TNA Women's Knockout Championship</a>, injuring her,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp1905_32-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp1905-32">[32]</a></sup> and unsuccessfully attempting to shave ODB's head after a match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp2305_33-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp2305-33">[33]</a></sup> This led to a Street Fight on June 5 between Sky and ODB, during which <a href="/wiki/Mickie_Knuckles" title="Mickie Knuckles">Mickie Knuckles</a> (later renamed Moose) debuted as The Beautiful People's ally on <i>Impact!</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp0606_34-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp0606-34">[34]</a></sup> At <a href="/wiki/Slammiversary_(2008)" title="Slammiversary (2008)">Slammiversary</a> the new trio lost in a six-woman tag team match against Roxxi, ODB and Kim when ODB pinned Moose.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-slam08_35-0"><a href="#cite_note-slam08-35">[35]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-slamlove_36-0"><a href="#cite_note-slamlove-36">[36]</a></sup></p>
<p>On July 18, Sky won a ten-Knockout Battle Royal to earn a shot at the Knockouts Championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp1807_37-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp1807-37">[37]</a></sup> However she failed to win the match, afterwards her and Love assaulted champion <a href="/wiki/Taylor_Wilde" title="Taylor Wilde">Taylor Wilde</a>, putting a paper bag over her head.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp2507_38-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp2507-38">[38]</a></sup> Their bad luck continued when The Beautiful People main evented the July 31 <i>Impact!</i> in a losing effort to Wilde and Kim.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp0108_39-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp0108-39">[39]</a></sup></p>
<p>On the August 14 edition of <i>Impact!</i>, <a href="/wiki/Billy_Gunn" title="Billy Gunn">Kip James</a> was introduced as the team's "<a href="/wiki/Fashion_design" title="Fashion design">fashionist</a>" under the name Cute Kip.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1508imp_40-0"><a href="#cite_note-1508imp-40">[40]</a></sup> As Sky had failed to win the title from Wilde, Love was given a chance at <a href="/wiki/No_Surrender_(2008)" title="No Surrender (2008)">No Surrender</a>. The following week on <i>Impact!</i>, The Beautiful People tried to intimidate Wilde before No Surrender, by attacking her backstage.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp2208_41-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp2208-41">[41]</a></sup> Love and Wilde competed in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Beauty_contest" title="Beauty contest">beauty pageant</a> which Love lost after losing the evening gown and talent contest segments.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp1209_42-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp1209-42">[42]</a></sup> Love also lost the title match at No Surrender.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nos08_43-0"><a href="#cite_note-nos08-43">[43]</a></sup> While Sky and Love had been focussing on Wilde and her title, Kip had begun a feud with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rhino_(wrestler)" title="Rhino (wrestler)">Rhino</a>. This feud ended in defeat for the Beautiful People, with them losing to ODB, <a href="/wiki/Trenesha_Biggers" title="Trenesha Biggers">Rhaka Khan</a> and Rhino at <a href="/wiki/Bound_for_Glory_IV" title="Bound for Glory IV">Bound for Glory IV</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bfg4_44-0"><a href="#cite_note-bfg4-44">[44]</a></sup> Their feud with ODB spilled out into an alliance with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Booker_Huffman" title="Booker Huffman">Booker T</a> who hired The Beautiful People to protect his wife, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sharmell_Sullivan-Huffman" title="Sharmell Sullivan-Huffman">Sharmell</a>, from ODB in exchange for his locker room on the December 4 episode of <i>Impact!</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp0512_45-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp0512-45">[45]</a></sup> This resulted in a six-woman tag team match at <a href="/wiki/Final_Resolution_(December_2008)" title="Final Resolution (December 2008)">Final Resolution</a> against ODB, Wilde and Roxxi, which they lost.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fs08_46-0"><a href="#cite_note-fs08-46">[46]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mi_Pi_Sexy_at_Destination_X.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="471" data-file-width="720" height="144" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Mi_Pi_Sexy_at_Destination_X.jpg/220px-Mi_Pi_Sexy_at_Destination_X.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Mi_Pi_Sexy_at_Destination_X.jpg/330px-Mi_Pi_Sexy_at_Destination_X.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Mi_Pi_Sexy_at_Destination_X.jpg/440px-Mi_Pi_Sexy_at_Destination_X.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mi_Pi_Sexy_at_Destination_X.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Madison_Rayne" title="Madison Rayne">Madison Rayne</a> (left) joined in March 2009 to make the sorority Mi∇⦵ (Mi Pi Sexy)</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Also in December it was announced on TNA's website that the company had extended an invitation to United States Vice-Presidential candidate <a href="/wiki/Sarah_Palin" title="Sarah Palin">Sarah Palin</a> which The Beautiful People looked forward to as they considered her husband to be attractive.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp2811_47-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp2811-47">[47]</a></sup> A Governor Palin parody character, often referred to simply as The Governor, appeared on December 4 played by <a href="/wiki/Daffney" title="Daffney">Shannon Spruill</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp0512_45-1"><a href="#cite_note-imp0512-45">[45]</a></sup> Love and Sky were oblivious to The Governor being an imposter, resulting in some comedy skits where Kip tried to convince them they were being fooled while others mocked their stupidity. The Governor, meanwhile, convinced the duo that they would have a makeover that would make them worthy of her cabinet; the makeover involved frumpy clothes, no make-up and unstyled hair. On January 15, Taylor Wilde and Roxxi revealed that it had all been a ruse to humiliate The Beautiful People who, in Wilde's opinion, were making a mockery of TNA's women's division. After this they had mud dropped on them from the ceiling.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp1501_48-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp1501-48">[48]</a></sup> The following week, The Beautiful People brutally attacked Spruill backstage until Kip stopped them after a sufficient beating.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp2301_49-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp2301-49">[49]</a></sup> On February 5, The Beautiful People exacted revenge on Roxxi and Wilde in a tag match and put paper bags over their heads; however, their revenge was cut short when The Governor made the save.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp0602_50-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp0602-50">[50]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Angelina_Love.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="453" data-file-width="604" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Angelina_Love.jpg/220px-Angelina_Love.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Angelina_Love.jpg/330px-Angelina_Love.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Angelina_Love.jpg/440px-Angelina_Love.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Angelina_Love.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Love in April 2009</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Wilde's rivalry with The Beautiful People continued when Wilde teamed with the recently debuted Knockout <a href="/wiki/Madison_Rayne" title="Madison Rayne">Madison Rayne</a> on February 26. Rayne turned on Wilde in the tag team match giving The Beautiful People the win.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp2702_51-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp2702-51">[51]</a></sup> With Rayne's help, The Beautiful People won a Four Corners Tag Team match against <a href="/wiki/Kia_Stevens" title="Kia Stevens">Awesome Kong</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cheerleader_Melissa" title="Cheerleader Melissa">Raisha Saeed</a>, <a href="/wiki/Trenesha_Biggers" title="Trenesha Biggers">Rhaka Khan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Josette_Bynum" title="Josette Bynum">Sojourner Bolt</a>, and Wilde and Roxxi.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp0603_52-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp0603-52">[52]</a></sup> On the March 12 edition of <i>Impact!</i>, Madison Rayne was formally revealed as an initiate to Mi Pi Sexy (Mi∇⦵) (the newly formed <a href="/wiki/Fraternities_and_sororities" title="Fraternities and sororities">sorority</a> of the group).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IGN_54-0"><a href="#cite_note-IGN-54">[54]</a></sup> However, Rayne lost her initiation match to Taylor Wilde.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp1303_55-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp1303-55">[55]</a></sup> Love and Sky continued to be referred to as "The Beautiful People", but when Rayne accompanied them, they were referred to as "Mi Pi Sexy". Some time later, the term "Mi Pi Sexy" became a nickname, thus being used occasionally on television.</p>
<p>The Beautiful People began the <a href="/wiki/Fraternities_and_sororities#Controversy_and_criticism" title="Fraternities and sororities">hazing</a> of Madison Rayne on March 19's <i>Impact</i>, which began with her helping them clip The Governor's hair after Rayne lost her match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp1903_56-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp1903-56">[56]</a></sup> Mi Pi Sexy would fight against Wilde, Roxxi, and The Governor at <a href="/wiki/Destination_X_(2009)" title="Destination X (2009)">Destination X</a>. Despite the numbers being even with the acquisition of Rayne, The Beautiful People failed to defeat their opponents.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dx09_57-0"><a href="#cite_note-dx09-57">[57]</a></sup> Monty Sopp, who played Cute Kip, was removed from television prior to Destination X to become a road agent, meaning his departure from the stable. This was explained on-screen by Sky, who stated that Kip was on probation before declaring he would be spoken about no more.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup></p>
<p>Rayne's hazing continued after The Beautiful People won an <i>Impact!</i> tag team match against Kong and Saeed, after which Rayne tried to cut the braided hair of the Knockout Champion Kong.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp2703_59-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp2703-59">[59]</a></sup> With Sky in her corner, Angelina Love faced Kong and perennial nemesis Taylor Wilde in a three-way cage match for the Knockout Championship at <a href="/wiki/Lockdown_(2009)" title="Lockdown (2009)">Lockdown</a>. Love narrowly escaped a somersault leg drop from Kong, and as she was recovering Love pushed her towards the cage while Sky pulled her frayed hair through the holes in the cage and tied her to it. With Kong unable to move from the cage, Wilde dove onto Love with a cross body press and legitimately knocked her unconscious with her knee. As she recovered, Wilde attacked Kong, allowing Love to roll-up Wilde for the pin and win the Knockout Championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lock09_60-0"><a href="#cite_note-lock09-60">[60]</a></sup> The following week on <i>Impact!</i>, Mi Pi Sexy had a celebration with male dancers and named Madison Rayne an official member of the Beautiful People. However the celebration was cut short by Kong.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp2404_61-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp2404-61">[61]</a></sup> Kong continued her attack on Mi Pi Sexy and proved her dominance by making her way through Rayne, Sky and Kip, who Love brought back to stop her, in <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_match_types#Container-based_variations" title="Professional wrestling match types">stretcher matches</a> on the following weeks of <i>Impact!</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp0105_62-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp0105-62">[62]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp0805_63-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp0805-63">[63]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp1505_64-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp1505-64">[64]</a></sup> Despite this, at <a href="/wiki/Sacrifice_(2009)" title="Sacrifice (2009)">Sacrifice</a> Love retained her title against Kong.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sac09_65-0"><a href="#cite_note-sac09-65">[65]</a></sup></p>
<p>On May 28, Love defended her title again against Sojourner Bolt with all of her associates at ringside. After quickly defeating Bolt, Love questioned why Cute Kip was still appearing with them and officially fired him from the group. After this Love made a speech about the dominance of The Beautiful People and mocked the lack of competition in TNA. This led to the debut of <a href="/wiki/Lisa_Marie_Varon" title="Lisa Marie Varon">Tara</a> who laid out both Sky and Rayne and used her <a href="/wiki/Neckbreaker#Gory_neckbreaker" title="Neckbreaker">Widow's Peak</a> finisher on Love, before accepting the challenge.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp2905_66-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp2905-66">[66]</a></sup> At <a href="/wiki/Slammiversary_(2009)" title="Slammiversary (2009)">Slammiversary</a>, Tara had her chance at the title but with the help of some hairspray from Sky and Rayne, Love retained the championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-slam09_67-0"><a href="#cite_note-slam09-67">[67]</a></sup> Tara, whose name alludes to the <a href="/wiki/Tarantula" title="Tarantula">tarantula</a> spider, began taunting the group with tarantulas over the next few weeks on <i>Impact!</i>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp2606_68-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp2606-68">[68]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp0307_69-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp0307-69">[69]</a></sup> which resulted in Sky voicing her frustration about Love leaving her alone with the tarantula and threatening to leave the group, if Love didn't back her up.</p>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kicked_out_of_the_club_by_KnightNephrite.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="960" data-file-width="1280" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Kicked_out_of_the_club_by_KnightNephrite.jpg/220px-Kicked_out_of_the_club_by_KnightNephrite.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Kicked_out_of_the_club_by_KnightNephrite.jpg/330px-Kicked_out_of_the_club_by_KnightNephrite.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Kicked_out_of_the_club_by_KnightNephrite.jpg/440px-Kicked_out_of_the_club_by_KnightNephrite.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Kicked_out_of_the_club_by_KnightNephrite.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Love and Sky evicting Rayne from The Beautiful People</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Consequently, when Tara defeated Sky and threatened to place a tarantula on her, Love agreed to put her Knockout Championship on the line immediately afterwards, and without Rayne for support, Love lost the championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp1007_70-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp1007-70">[70]</a></sup> The following week Love demanded, and gained a rematch but was laid out with the Widow's Peak from Tara.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp1707_71-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp1707-71">[71]</a></sup> At <a href="/wiki/Victory_Road_(2009)" title="Victory Road (2009)">Victory Road</a>, Love almost lost her match when she was accidentally blinded with hairspray, but kicked out and later pinned Tara despite her foot being under the bottom rope, to win back the Knockout Championship. Later in the evening the referee was seen leaving Rayne's shower, with the implication she had seduced him to officiate the match in Love's favour.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-vicr09_72-0"><a href="#cite_note-vicr09-72">[72]</a></sup></p>
<p>After all three failed to win a Battle Royal to become a member of <a href="/wiki/The_Main_Event_Mafia" title="The Main Event Mafia">Main Event Mafia</a>, the group were seen mocking ODB and her associate <a href="/wiki/Cody_Deaner" title="Cody Deaner">Cody Deaner</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp2407_73-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp2407-73">[73]</a></sup> A six-woman tag team match between all of Mi Pi Sexy against Tara, Kong and ODB turned into a three-on-one handicap match when Tara and Kong began to brawl between themselves. After a kiss from Deaner at ringside, Love was stunned and lost the match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imp3107_74-0"><a href="#cite_note-imp3107-74">[74]</a></sup> It was later announced that at <a href="/wiki/Hard_Justice_(2009)" title="Hard Justice (2009)">Hard Justice</a>, the Knockout Championship would be on the line in a tag team contest between The Beautiful People against ODB and Deaner. After more mistimed hairspraying from Rayne, ODB won the title by virtue of Deaner pinning Sky.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-hj09_75-0"><a href="#cite_note-hj09-75">[75]</a></sup> On the August 20 edition of <i>Impact!</i>, Madison Rayne was kicked out of Mi Pi Sexy for costing Love the title, being assaulted and paper bagged by them.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76"><a href="#cite_note-76">[76]</a></sup></p>
<p>On September 3, 2009, Williams was released from TNA due to visa issues, while still a top draw in the women's division.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77"><a href="#cite_note-77">[77]</a></sup> However, on September 7, 2009, Williams posted a blog entry on her MySpace account stating that she would return to TNA Wrestling once the issues with her visa were sorted out.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup> She continued appearing on <i>Impact!</i> for two more weeks due to the tapings being held before her release. In the episodes she and Velvet Sky advanced to the finals of the tournament for the <a href="/wiki/TNA_Knockouts_Tag_Team_Championship" title="TNA Knockouts Tag Team Championship">TNA Knockouts Tag Team Championship</a> with help from Madison Rayne, whom they afterwards welcomed to return to the Beautiful People.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79"><a href="#cite_note-79">[79]</a></sup> Rayne would go on to replace Love in the finals for the Knockouts Tag Team Championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80"><a href="#cite_note-80">[80]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Women_Superstars_Uncensored_.282009.E2.80.932010.29">Women Superstars Uncensored (2009–2010)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Women Superstars Uncensored (2009–2010)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>After her release from TNA, Williams began working for <a href="/wiki/Women_Superstars_Uncensored" title="Women Superstars Uncensored">Women Superstars Uncensored</a> (WSU), where she performed under her TNA ring name of Angelina Love. On November 14, 2009, she unsuccessfully challenged <a href="/wiki/Mercedes_Martinez" title="Mercedes Martinez">Mercedes Martinez</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Women_Superstars_Uncensored#WSU_Championship" title="Women Superstars Uncensored">WSU Championship</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81"><a href="#cite_note-81">[81]</a></sup> On December 12 she teamed with Jennifer Cruz to defeat Jana and Rick Cataldo in a tag team match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82"><a href="#cite_note-82">[82]</a></sup> After returning to TNA, Williams made one more appearance for WSU, defeating <a href="/wiki/Sassy_Stephie" title="Sassy Stephie">Sassy Stephie</a> at the 3rd Anniversary Show on March 6, 2010.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-26"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_return_to_TNA">Second return to TNA</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Second return to TNA">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Feud_with_The_Beautiful_People_.282010.29">Feud with The Beautiful People (2010)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Feud with The Beautiful People (2010)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:AngelinaLove1.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2304" data-file-width="1728" height="227" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/AngelinaLove1.JPG/170px-AngelinaLove1.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/AngelinaLove1.JPG/255px-AngelinaLove1.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/AngelinaLove1.JPG/340px-AngelinaLove1.JPG 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:AngelinaLove1.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Love as the <a href="/wiki/TNA_Knockouts_Championship" title="TNA Knockouts Championship">TNA Knockouts Champion</a>, wearing an anti-Beautiful People T-shirt</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>On January 2, 2010, it was reported that Williams had re-signed with TNA.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83"><a href="#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup> Williams, as Angelina Love, made her return on the January 14 episode of <i>Impact!</i>, appearing in the crowd and hugging Velvet Sky and Madison Rayne prior to their match with Awesome Kong and <a href="/wiki/Ayako_Hamada" title="Ayako Hamada">Hamada</a>. However, after the match, Love turned <a href="/wiki/Face_(professional_wrestling)" title="Face (professional wrestling)">face</a> by attacking her former partners and <a href="/wiki/Lacey_Von_Erich" title="Lacey Von Erich">Lacey Von Erich</a>, her replacement in the group, seemingly angry about being replaced.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Jan14_84-0"><a href="#cite_note-Jan14-84">[84]</a></sup> She made her in-ring return the following week by defeating Rayne, however after the match she was triple teamed by the Beautiful People.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-In-RingReturnTNA_85-0"><a href="#cite_note-In-RingReturnTNA-85">[85]</a></sup> On the February 4 episode of <i>Impact!</i> she was unsuccessful in her attempt to regain the Knockout Championship from Tara.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReturnTitle_86-0"><a href="#cite_note-ReturnTitle-86">[86]</a></sup> On the March 8 episode of <i>Impact!</i> Love and Tara teamed up to challenge for the vacant Knockouts Tag Team Championship, but were defeated by Rayne and Sky, after interference from <a href="/wiki/Daffney" title="Daffney">Daffney</a>, with whom Tara was involved in a feud.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87"><a href="#cite_note-87">[87]</a></sup></p>
<p>On the April 5 episode of <i>Impact!</i>, Love teamed with Tara, ODB, and Hamada to face the Beautiful People and Daffney in the first ever Lockbox elimination match, contested for four keys to four boxes containing prizes. Love won a key by eliminating Lacey Von Erich, and it was later revealed that her key opened the box, which contained the Knockout Championship, making her a three-time champion.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup> After Love won the title, friction developed between her and Tara heading into their upcoming match against The Beautiful People, with Tara slowly turning villainous. At <a href="/wiki/Lockdown_(2010)" title="Lockdown (2010)">Lockdown</a>, Love lost the Knockouts Championship to Madison Rayne, after she pinned Tara in a tag team <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_match_types#Cages" title="Professional wrestling match types">steel cage match</a>, where Love and Tara faced Rayne and Velvet Sky for both the Women's Knockout Championship and the Knockouts Tag Team Championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lockdown2010_89-0"><a href="#cite_note-Lockdown2010-89">[89]</a></sup> After the match, Love was attacked by the evil Tara, who turned villainous in the process.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lockdown2010_89-1"><a href="#cite_note-Lockdown2010-89">[89]</a></sup> At the April 20 tapings of <i>Impact!</i>, Williams partially tore her biceps and suffered ligament damage in her arm and was expected to be out of action until May.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90"><a href="#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup> On May 26 it was announced that Williams had been cleared to return to wrestling.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Angelina_Love_July_2010.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1152" data-file-width="1728" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/Angelina_Love_July_2010.jpg/220px-Angelina_Love_July_2010.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/Angelina_Love_July_2010.jpg/330px-Angelina_Love_July_2010.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/Angelina_Love_July_2010.jpg/440px-Angelina_Love_July_2010.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Angelina_Love_July_2010.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Love in July 2010</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>When Love returned from her injury on the June 17 episode of <i>Impact!</i>, she vowed to reclaim the Knockouts title and stated that she would go through each member of the Beautiful People to do it. That night she faced Von Erich and got disqualified after dropping her with a <a href="/wiki/DDT_(professional_wrestling)" title="DDT (professional wrestling)">DDT</a> on a steel chair.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wicked-DT_92-0"><a href="#cite_note-Wicked-DT-92">[92]</a></sup> The following week her match with Velvet Sky ended in similar fashion.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wicked-DT2_93-0"><a href="#cite_note-Wicked-DT2-93">[93]</a></sup> On July 11 at <a href="/wiki/Victory_Road_(2010)" title="Victory Road (2010)">Victory Road</a>, Love defeated Rayne via disqualification in a <a href="/wiki/Lucha_libre#Luchas_de_Apuestas" title="Lucha libre">Title vs. Career match</a> to win the Women's Knockout Championship for the fourth time. Prior to the match it was announced that the title would change hands via disqualification, if either Velvet Sky or Lacey Von Erich interfered in the match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-VictoryRoad2010_94-0"><a href="#cite_note-VictoryRoad2010-94">[94]</a></sup> However, the title was returned to Rayne on the July 22 episode of <i>Impact!</i>, when it was declared that there was no proof that the person who had interfered in the match was either Sky or Von Erich.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95"><a href="#cite_note-95">[95]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96"><a href="#cite_note-96">[96]</a></sup> The following week Love defeated <a href="/wiki/Sarah_Stock" title="Sarah Stock">Sarita</a> to once again become the number one contender to Rayne's title.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97"><a href="#cite_note-97">[97]</a></sup> Two weeks later Love defeated Rayne, after a distraction from Velvet Sky, to win the Women's Knockout Championship for the fifth time.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98"><a href="#cite_note-98">[98]</a></sup></p>
<p>On the August 19 episode of Impact!, Love reunited with Velvet Sky, who accompanied her to the ring, when she successfully defended her Women's Knockout Championship in a rematch against Rayne, who was with the mysterious biker woman. After the match Love and Sky were attacked by Rayne and the biker.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99"><a href="#cite_note-99">[99]</a></sup> Rayne's mysterious ally was finally unmasked as Tara on the September 2 episode of <i>Impact!</i>, when the two of them defeated Love and Sky in their first match together in a year.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100"><a href="#cite_note-100">[100]</a></sup> On the September 16 edition of <i>Impact!</i> Love and Sky saved Lacey Von Erich, who was making a return from her injury, from a beating at the hands of Rayne and Tara and accepted her back into The Beautiful People.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101"><a href="#cite_note-101">[101]</a></sup> She, however, would leave the promotion two months later on November 11.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102"><a href="#cite_note-102">[102]</a></sup> During the feud Rayne had claimed to own the rights to the name the Beautiful People, but on the October 7 live edition of <i>Impact!</i>, Love and Sky defeated her and Tara in a tag team match to officially earn the right to call themselves the Beautiful People.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Impact082610_103-0"><a href="#cite_note-Impact082610-103">[103]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Impact100710_104-0"><a href="#cite_note-Impact100710-104">[104]</a></sup> On October 10 at <a href="/wiki/Bound_for_Glory_(2010)" title="Bound for Glory (2010)">Bound for Glory</a> Love lost the Women's Knockout Championship to Tara in a Four Corners match, which also included Velvet Sky and Madison Rayne and was refereed by Mickie James.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105"><a href="#cite_note-105">[105]</a></sup></p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Storyline_with_Winter_and_Knockouts_Tag_Team_Champion_.282010.E2.80.932012.29">Storyline with Winter and Knockouts Tag Team Champion (2010–2012)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Storyline with Winter and Knockouts Tag Team Champion (2010–2012)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Love_Winter_champs!.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3264" data-file-width="2448" height="227" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Love_Winter_champs%21.jpg/170px-Love_Winter_champs%21.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Love_Winter_champs%21.jpg/255px-Love_Winter_champs%21.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Love_Winter_champs%21.jpg/340px-Love_Winter_champs%21.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Love_Winter_champs!.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Love and <a href="/wiki/Katarina_Waters" title="Katarina Waters">Winter</a> as the <a href="/wiki/TNA_Knockouts_Tag_Team_Championship" title="TNA Knockouts Tag Team Championship">TNA Knockouts Tag Team Champions</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>On the October 21 episode of <i>Impact!</i> Love entered a storyline where a woman named <a href="/wiki/Katarina_Waters" title="Katarina Waters">Winter</a> started appearing in mirrors, claiming to be her fan, though only Love was able to see her.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106"><a href="#cite_note-106">[106]</a></sup> After weeks of appearing only in front of Love, Winter was for the first time seen by the other people on the November 25 episode of <i>Impact!</i>, when she saved Love during a large backstage brawl.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107"><a href="#cite_note-107">[107]</a></sup> On the December 9 episode of <i>Impact!</i> Love and Sky entered a four–team tournament for the vacated Knockouts Tag Team Championship, defeating Sarita and Daffney in their first round match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108"><a href="#cite_note-108">[108]</a></sup> On the December 23 episode of <i>Impact!</i>, Winter replaced an injured Velvet Sky, who had been attacked by Sarita, in the tournament final and teamed with Love to defeat Madison Rayne and Tara for the TNA Knockouts Tag Team Championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Impact122310Tapings_109-0"><a href="#cite_note-Impact122310Tapings-109">[109]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Impact122310_110-0"><a href="#cite_note-Impact122310-110">[110]</a></sup></p>
<p>On the January 13 edition of <i>Impact!</i>, Angelina and Winter successfully defend their championship against Madison Rayne and Tara after Winter knocked out Tara with a dragon sleeper.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111"><a href="#cite_note-111">[111]</a></sup> On the January 27 edition of <i>Impact!</i>, Winter brawled with Velvet Sky, who claimed she was trying to break up <a href="/wiki/The_Beautiful_People_(professional_wrestling)" title="The Beautiful People (professional wrestling)">The Beautiful People</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112"><a href="#cite_note-112">[112]</a></sup> On the March 3 edition of <i>Impact!</i>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rebecca_Bayless" title="Rebecca Bayless">Cookie</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rob_Strauss" title="Rob Strauss">Robbie E</a> aligned themselves with former <i><a href="/wiki/Jersey_Shore_(TV_series)" title="Jersey Shore (TV series)">Jersey Shore</a></i> cast member <a href="/wiki/Angelina_Pivarnick" title="Angelina Pivarnick">Angelina Pivarnick</a>, with whom they bonded through their mutual dislike of <a href="/wiki/JWoww" title="JWoww">Jenni "JWoww" Farley</a>, whom Pivarnick proceeded to challenge to a match (whom was replaced by Winter).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113"><a href="#cite_note-113">[113]</a></sup> The following week, Love, <a href="/wiki/Velvet_Sky" title="Velvet Sky">Velvet Sky</a> and Winter defeated Cookie, Angelina Pivarnick and <a href="/wiki/Sarah_Stock" title="Sarah Stock">Sarita</a> in a six knockout tag team match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114"><a href="#cite_note-114">[114]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:AngelinaLoveSignatureEntrance.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3264" data-file-width="2448" height="227" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/AngelinaLoveSignatureEntrance.jpg/170px-AngelinaLoveSignatureEntrance.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/AngelinaLoveSignatureEntrance.jpg/255px-AngelinaLoveSignatureEntrance.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/AngelinaLoveSignatureEntrance.jpg/340px-AngelinaLoveSignatureEntrance.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:AngelinaLoveSignatureEntrance.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Love at a TNA <a href="/wiki/House_show" title="House show">live event</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>On March 13, 2011, at <a href="/wiki/Victory_Road_(2011)" title="Victory Road (2011)">Victory Road</a>, Love and Winter lost the Knockouts Tag Team Championship to Sarita and <a href="/wiki/Thea_Trinidad" title="Thea Trinidad">Rosita</a>, after an interference by Velvet Sky backfired.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115"><a href="#cite_note-115">[115]</a></sup> On the March 24 episode of <i>Impact!</i>, Winter, seemingly having control over Love's actions, prevented her from saving Sky from a beatdown at the hands of Sarita and Rosita.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116"><a href="#cite_note-116">[116]</a></sup> Love was kept under Winter's spell with drinks of what she described as her medicine.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Impact040711_117-0"><a href="#cite_note-Impact040711-117">[117]</a></sup> On the April 7 episode of <i>Impact!</i>, Love turned heel by attacking Sky during a Knockouts Tag Team Championship match against Sarita and Rosita and left her to be pinned by the champions.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Impact040711_117-1"><a href="#cite_note-Impact040711-117">[117]</a></sup> On the April 28 episode of <i>Impact!</i>, Love defeated Sky via submission in a singles match, <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_professional_wrestling_terms#No-sell" title="Glossary of professional wrestling terms">no-selling</a> all of her opponent's offense during the match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RearNeck_118-0"><a href="#cite_note-RearNeck-118">[118]</a></sup> On the May 5 episode of <i>Impact!</i>, Sky gained a measure of revenge on her former partner, when she teamed with <a href="/wiki/Kurt_Angle" title="Kurt Angle">Kurt Angle</a> in a handicap mixed tag team match, where they defeated Love, Winter and <a href="/wiki/Jeff_Jarrett" title="Jeff Jarrett">Jeff Jarrett</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-119"><a href="#cite_note-119">[119]</a></sup> The feud between the former Beautiful People partners seemingly ended on the May 19 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, with Sky defeating Love and Winter in a handicap match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-120"><a href="#cite_note-120">[120]</a></sup></p>
<p>The following week Love attacked Mickie James, after she had defeated Winter in a singles match, setting up a match between the two for the TNA Women's Knockout Championship at <a href="/wiki/Slammiversary_IX" title="Slammiversary IX">Slammiversary IX</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-121"><a href="#cite_note-121">[121]</a></sup> Prior to the match at the pay-per-view, Love declined to take her medicine, saying that she no longer needed it as she now understood Winter. After failing in her attempt to win the title, both Love and Winter attacked James.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-122"><a href="#cite_note-122">[122]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-123"><a href="#cite_note-123">[123]</a></sup> On the June 23 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Love helped Winter defeat James in a non-title <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_match_types#Hardcore-based_variations" title="Professional wrestling match types">Street Fight</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Impact062311_124-0"><a href="#cite_note-Impact062311-124">[124]</a></sup> On August 7 at <a href="/wiki/Hardcore_Justice_(2011)" title="Hardcore Justice (2011)">Hardcore Justice</a>, Love again helped Winter defeat James, this time to become the new Women's Knockout Champion.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-125"><a href="#cite_note-125">[125]</a></sup> On the September 15 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Love failed to earn a shot at the title as she was defeated by Velvet Sky in a qualifying match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126"><a href="#cite_note-126">[126]</a></sup></p>
<p>After being inactive for two months, Love returned on the January 19 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, challenging Eric Young to a match. Young won the match via disqualification, after Love kicked him in the groin.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127"><a href="#cite_note-127">[127]</a></sup> On the January 26 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Love and Winter lost to ODB and Eric Young in a tag team match, this was Love and Winter's last appearance together as a team.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128"><a href="#cite_note-128">[128]</a></sup> Love competed in a ten knockout battle royal for the number one contendership for Gail Kim's Knockout Championship on the February 16 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, but was defeated by Madison Rayne.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129"><a href="#cite_note-129">[129]</a></sup> Love wrestled, what turned out to be her final <i>Impact Wrestling</i> match, on the April 5 episode, where she was defeated in a six-way number one contender's match by Velvet Sky.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LastTVMatch_130-0"><a href="#cite_note-LastTVMatch-130">[130]</a></sup> On June 14, at a TNA <a href="/wiki/House_show" title="House show">house show</a> in <a href="/wiki/Belton,_Texas" title="Belton, Texas">Belton, Texas</a>, Love teamed up with Winter for the first time in almost five months, when the two, Rosita and Sarita were defeated in a four-on-three handicap main event by Mickie James, Tara and Velvet Sky.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131"><a href="#cite_note-131">[131]</a></sup> Two days later at another house show in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Houston,_Texas" title="Houston, Texas">Houston, Texas</a>, Love wrestled her final TNA match, where she and Winter were defeated by Tara and Velvet Sky, when Tara pinned Love.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132"><a href="#cite_note-132">[132]</a></sup></p>
<p>On July 1, 2012, Williams announced on her <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">Twitter</a> page that she had been granted her release from TNA.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133"><a href="#cite_note-133">[133]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134"><a href="#cite_note-134">[134]</a></sup> Angelina would also turn down an offer to return to the company in March 2013 as TNA reached out for her to appear at a one night all <a href="/wiki/TNA_Knockout" title="TNA Knockout">TNA Knockouts</a> <a href="/wiki/Pay-per-view" title="Pay-per-view">PPV</a> event.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-turns_down_ppv_135-0"><a href="#cite_note-turns_down_ppv-135">[135]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Third_return_to_TNA">Third return to TNA</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Third return to TNA">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Beautiful_People_reunion_.282014.E2.80.932016.29">The Beautiful People reunion (2014–2016)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: The Beautiful People reunion (2014–2016)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/The_Beautiful_People_(professional_wrestling)" title="The Beautiful People (professional wrestling)">The Beautiful People</a></div>
<p>It was announced by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Total_Nonstop_Action" title="Total Nonstop Action">TNA</a> that a former <a href="/wiki/TNA_Knockouts_Championship" title="TNA Knockouts Championship">TNA Women's Knockout Champion</a> was signed to a contract and would be returning, which would later be revealed to be Love.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136"><a href="#cite_note-136">[136]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137"><a href="#cite_note-137">[137]</a></sup> Love made her return to TNA on the March 13, 2014 episode of <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/TNA_Impact!" title="TNA Impact!">Impact Wrestling</a></i>, calling out <a href="/wiki/Velvet_Sky" title="Velvet Sky">Velvet Sky</a> wanting to reunite <a href="/wiki/The_Beautiful_People_(professional_wrestling)" title="The Beautiful People (professional wrestling)">The Beautiful People</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Carapola_138-0"><a href="#cite_note-Carapola-138">[138]</a></sup> Sky would later accept Love's offer on the March 20 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, while <a href="/wiki/Madison_Rayne" title="Madison Rayne">Madison Rayne</a> declined due to Love's attitude towards her. Later in the show, Love attacked Rayne, after the two hugged, establishing herself as a <a href="/wiki/Heel_(professional_wrestling)" title="Heel (professional wrestling)">heel</a> in the process.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Carapola_138-1"><a href="#cite_note-Carapola-138">[138]</a></sup> On the March 27 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Love defeated Rayne in her returning match due to interference from Sky, who also turned heel, officially returning the original heel incarnation of the stable.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BFFs_139-0"><a href="#cite_note-BFFs-139">[139]</a></sup> The Beautiful People made their in-ring return the following week on <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, defeating Rayne and <a href="/wiki/Santana_Garrett" title="Santana Garrett">Brittany</a>, when Love pinned Brittany after a modified <i>Makeover</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReturnofBPs_140-0"><a href="#cite_note-ReturnofBPs-140">[140]</a></sup> On the April 10 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Love defeated <a href="/wiki/ODB_(wrestler)" title="ODB (wrestler)">ODB</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gail_Kim" title="Gail Kim">Gail Kim</a> and Brittany in a fatal four-way match to become the number one contender to Rayne's Women's Knockout Championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141"><a href="#cite_note-141">[141]</a></sup> Later, it was announced that Love suffered a legitimate <a href="/wiki/Concussion" title="Concussion">concussion</a> during the match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142"><a href="#cite_note-142">[142]</a></sup></p>
<p>On the April 24 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, The Beautiful People would once again defeat Rayne in a tag team match, only this time with Gail Kim as her partner.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143"><a href="#cite_note-143">[143]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144"><a href="#cite_note-144">[144]</a></sup> Three days later, at the <a href="/wiki/Sacrifice_(2014)" title="Sacrifice (2014)">Sacrifice</a> pay-per-view on April 27, Love defeated Rayne to become a six-time Knockouts Champion, her first reign since 2010.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6KnockoutsTitle_145-0"><a href="#cite_note-6KnockoutsTitle-145">[145]</a></sup> Kim joined the feud after interrupting Love's title celebration which led to Rayne and Brittany stripping The Beautiful People of their evening gowns.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146"><a href="#cite_note-146">[146]</a></sup> This led to a <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_tag_team_match_types#Elimination_tag_team_matches" title="Professional wrestling tag team match types">tag team elimination</a> <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_match_types#Evening_Gown" title="Professional wrestling match types">evening gown</a> match on the May 8 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, which The Beautiful People won.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147"><a href="#cite_note-147">[147]</a></sup> In her first title defense, on the May 22 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Love defeated Brittany in an open-challenge match. After the match, Love and Sky would attack Brittany and Gail Kim would make the save.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148"><a href="#cite_note-148">[148]</a></sup> This led to a tag team match, where The Beautiful People defeated Kim and Brittany on the May 29 edition of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup> Love and Kim would finally face off in a title match on June 15 at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Slammiversary_(2014)" title="Slammiversary (2014)">Slammiversary</a> pay-per-view, where Love would successfully defend her championship.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150"><a href="#cite_note-150">[150]</a></sup> On June 20, during the tapings of the July 3 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Love lost the Women's Knockout Championship to Kim, ending her reign at only 67 days.</p>
<p>On the July 10 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Love unsuccessfully challenged Gail Kim for the title in a four-way match also involving Madison Rayne and Brittany.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151"><a href="#cite_note-151">[151]</a></sup> The Beautiful People would interrupt a championship match between Kim and <a href="/wiki/Taryn_Terrell" title="Taryn Terrell">Taryn Terrell</a> on the July 24 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, leading to a no-contest.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup> This led to a four-way contest for the Women's Knockout Championship between the four women, in which Love was unsuccessful in regaining the title.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup> At <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hardcore_Justice_(2014)" title="Hardcore Justice (2014)">Hardcore Justice</a>, Love unsuccessfully challenged Kim for the title in a Last Knockout Standing match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup> In late 2014, The Beautiful People formed an alliance with <a href="/wiki/The_BroMans" title="The BroMans">The BroMans</a> and regularly teamed with them. On the January 23, 2015 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Velvet Sky retrieved a briefcase for <a href="/wiki/Robbie_E" title="Robbie E">Robbie E</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Feast_or_Fired" title="Feast or Fired">Feast or Fired</a> match. The briefcase contained the "pink" slip and Sky was fired, effectively disbanding The Beautiful People in the process.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup></p>
<p>Love then separated from <a href="/wiki/The_BroMans" title="The BroMans">The BroMans</a> after they disbanded in April 2015.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup> On the <i>TKO: Night of Knockouts</i> special episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i> on April 24, Love competed in a <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_match_types#Basic_non-elimination_matches" title="Professional wrestling match types">fatal four–way</a> number one contender's match against <a href="/wiki/Brooke_Tessmacher" title="Brooke Tessmacher">Brooke</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gail_Kim" title="Gail Kim">Gail Kim</a> and <a href="/wiki/Madison_Rayne" title="Madison Rayne">Madison Rayne</a>, which Brooke won.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157"><a href="#cite_note-157">[157]</a></sup> On the May 8 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, <a href="/wiki/Velvet_Sky" title="Velvet Sky">Velvet Sky</a> returned to TNA and attacked Love.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-James.2C_Bobby_158-0"><a href="#cite_note-James.2C_Bobby-158">[158]</a></sup> On the June 3 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Love got Sky arrested by her security staff after she attacked Madison Rayne, while Love was arrested herself by event staff as Sky appeared as a fan, and was arrested for fan assault.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159"><a href="#cite_note-159">[159]</a></sup> On the June 24 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Sky defeated Love to secure her spot on the roster.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160"><a href="#cite_note-160">[160]</a></sup></p>
