<p>On the September 2 episode of <i>Impact Wrestling</i>, Love and Madison Rayne came to the aid of <a href="/wiki/Velvet_Sky" title="Velvet Sky">Velvet Sky</a>, who was being beaten down by <a href="/wiki/The_Dollhouse_(professional_wrestling)" title="The Dollhouse (professional wrestling)">Dollhouse</a> members <a href="/wiki/Rebel_(wrestler)" title="Rebel (wrestler)">Rebel</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jade_(wrestler)" title="Jade (wrestler)">Jade</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marti_Bell" title="Marti Bell">Marti Bell</a>, turning <a href="/wiki/Face_(professional_wrestling)" title="Face (professional wrestling)">face</a> and reforming <a href="/wiki/The_Beautiful_People_(professional_wrestling)" title="The Beautiful People (professional wrestling)">The Beautiful People</a> in the process.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161"><a href="#cite_note-161">[161]</a></sup> The following week, The Beautiful People were attacked backstage by the Dollhouse, which resulted in Love breaking her arm in the <a href="/wiki/Kayfabe" title="Kayfabe">storyline</a>, writing her off television due to her <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_professional_wrestling_terms#Legit" title="Glossary of professional wrestling terms">legitimate</a> pregnancy.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162"><a href="#cite_note-162">[162]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163"><a href="#cite_note-163">[163]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164"><a href="#cite_note-164">[164]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165"><a href="#cite_note-165">[165]</a></sup> On March 27, 2016, Williams announced on her <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">Twitter</a> account that her contract with TNA had expired during the pregnancy.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166"><a href="#cite_note-166">[166]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-167"><a href="#cite_note-167">[167]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Independent_circuit_.282016.29">Return to Independent circuit (2016)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Return to Independent circuit (2016)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the month of June 2016 Love competed in a triple threat match involving <a href="/wiki/Rebel_(wrestler)" title="Rebel (wrestler)">Rebel</a> and <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Rocks-C_(wrestler)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Rocks-C (wrestler) (page does not exist)">Rocks-C</a> in which would win. On June 18, 2016 Love defeated <a href="/wiki/Veda_Scott" title="Veda Scott">Veda Scott</a> in a singles match.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fourth_return_to_TNA_.282017.E2.80.93present.29">Fourth return to TNA (2017–present)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Fourth return to TNA (2017–present)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/The_American_Wolves" title="The American Wolves">The American Wolves</a></div>
<p>On January 8, 2017, during the tapings for <a href="/wiki/TNA_One_Night_Only#Rivals_2017" title="TNA One Night Only">TNA One Night Only: Rivals 2017</a>, Love made her return to TNA, defeating <a href="/wiki/Madison_Rayne" title="Madison Rayne">Madison Rayne</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Williams identifies herself as a supporter of the <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Party_of_Canada" title="Liberal Party of Canada">Liberal Party of Canada</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168"><a href="#cite_note-168">[168]</a></sup> In late 2007, she began dating Jared Weeks, the lead singer of the band <a href="/wiki/Saving_Abel" title="Saving Abel">Saving Abel</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169"><a href="#cite_note-169">[169]</a></sup> but as of August 2008, the couple decided to split.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170"><a href="#cite_note-170">[170]</a></sup></p>
<p>In January 2015, Williams began dating fellow TNA wrestler <a href="/wiki/Davey_Richards" title="Davey Richards">Davey Richards</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171"><a href="#cite_note-171">[171]</a></sup> The couple announced their engagement on April 27, 2015,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172"><a href="#cite_note-172">[172]</a></sup> and were married on June 10, 2015.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-173"><a href="#cite_note-173">[173]</a></sup> On July 30, Williams announced on her <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">Twitter</a> account that she and Richards were expecting their first child,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174"><a href="#cite_note-174">[174]</a></sup> a boy named David Vincent Richards, born on March 17, 2016.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175"><a href="#cite_note-175">[175]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_media">Other media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Other media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Williams appeared on an episode of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Jenny_Jones_Show" title="The Jenny Jones Show">The Jenny Jones Show</a></i> about former "<a href="/wiki/Geek" title="Geek">geeks</a>" turned into physical competitors.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SLAMBio_9-1"><a href="#cite_note-SLAMBio-9">[9]</a></sup> She also made an appearance on <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kenny_vs_Spenny" title="Kenny vs Spenny">Kenny vs Spenny</a></i> in the episode "Who is the Strongest", alongside fellow <a href="/wiki/TNA_Knockout" title="TNA Knockout">TNA Knockout</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tracy_Brookshaw" title="Tracy Brookshaw">Traci Brooks</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SLAMBio_9-2"><a href="#cite_note-SLAMBio-9">[9]</a></sup> Williams played small roles in the 2008 film <i>CX2: The Movie</i>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imdb_176-0"><a href="#cite_note-imdb-176">[176]</a></sup> and in the 2010 <a href="/wiki/Independent_film" title="Independent film">indie</a> film <i>Good Intentions</i>, starring <a href="/wiki/LeAnn_Rimes" title="LeAnn Rimes">LeAnn Rimes</a> and <a href="/wiki/Luke_Perry" title="Luke Perry">Luke Perry</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177"><a href="#cite_note-177">[177]</a></sup> She was also featured on an episode of <a href="/wiki/MTV" title="MTV">MTV</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/Made_(TV_series)" title="Made (TV series)">Made</a></i>, alongside <a href="/wiki/A.J._Styles" title="A.J. Styles">A.J. Styles</a>, <a href="/wiki/Taylor_Wilde" title="Taylor Wilde">Taylor Wilde</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Velvet_Sky" title="Velvet Sky">Velvet Sky</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178"><a href="#cite_note-178">[178]</a></sup> On January 24, 2009, she appeared as a "soccerette" on British television program <i><a href="/wiki/Soccer_AM" title="Soccer AM">Soccer AM</a></i>, wearing a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Leeds_United" title="Leeds United">Leeds United</a> replica shirt, along with Velvet Sky.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-179"><a href="#cite_note-179">[179]</a></sup> In November 2010, she was a contestant on an all TNA week of <i><a href="/wiki/Family_Feud" title="Family Feud">Family Feud</a></i>, teaming with <a href="/wiki/Christy_Hemme" title="Christy Hemme">Christy Hemme</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lacey_Von_Erich" title="Lacey Von Erich">Lacey Von Erich</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lisa_Marie_Varon" title="Lisa Marie Varon">Tara</a> and Velvet Sky against <a href="/wiki/Jay_Lethal" title="Jay Lethal">Jay Lethal</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Matt_Morgan_(wrestler)" title="Matt Morgan (wrestler)">Matt Morgan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mick_Foley" title="Mick Foley">Mick Foley</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mr._Kennedy" title="Mr. Kennedy">Mr. Anderson</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rob_Van_Dam" title="Rob Van Dam">Rob Van Dam</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180"><a href="#cite_note-180">[180]</a></sup> Williams played the role of Rosemary Black in the 2011 <i><a href="/wiki/Dark_Rising" title="Dark Rising">Dark Rising</a></i> film <i><a href="/wiki/Dark_Rising#Dark_Rising:_Summer_Strikes_Back_.282011.29" title="Dark Rising">Dark Rising: Summer Strikes Back</a></i>, and the 2014 television series <i><a href="/wiki/Dark_Rising#Dark_Rising:_Warrior_of_Worlds_.282013.29" title="Dark Rising">Dark Rising: Warrior of Worlds</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-imdb_176-1"><a href="#cite_note-imdb-176">[176]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Championships_and_accomplishments">Championships and accomplishments</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Angelina_Love&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Championships and accomplishments">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Angelina_spraying_the_Fans.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="611" data-file-width="600" height="173" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Angelina_spraying_the_Fans.jpg/170px-Angelina_spraying_the_Fans.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Angelina_spraying_the_Fans.jpg/255px-Angelina_spraying_the_Fans.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Angelina_spraying_the_Fans.jpg/340px-Angelina_spraying_the_Fans.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Angelina_spraying_the_Fans.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Love is a six-time <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/TNA_Knockout_Championship" title="TNA Knockout Championship">TNA Knockouts Champion</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><i><b><a href="/wiki/Pro_Wrestling_Illustrated" title="Pro Wrestling Illustrated">Pro Wrestling Illustrated</a></b></i>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Pro_Wrestling_Illustrated_awards#Woman_of_the_Year" title="List of Pro Wrestling Illustrated awards">Woman of the Year</a> (2009, 2010)</li>
<li>Ranked her No. 2 of the top 50 female wrestlers in the <i><a href="/wiki/Pro_Wrestling_Illustrated#PWI_Female_50" title="Pro Wrestling Illustrated">PWI Female Top 50</a></i> in 2009<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pwi09_205-0"><a href="#cite_note-pwi09-205">[205]</a></sup> and in 2010<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pwi10_206-0"><a href="#cite_note-pwi10-206">[206]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Total_Nonstop_Action_Wrestling" title="Total Nonstop Action Wrestling">Total Nonstop Action Wrestling</a></b>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/TNA_Women%27s_Knockout_Championship" title="TNA Women's Knockout Championship">TNA Women's Knockout Championship</a> (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_TNA_Women%27s_Knockout_Champions#Title_history" title="List of TNA Women's Knockout Champions">6 times</a>)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OWOW_4-48"><a href="#cite_note-OWOW-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/TNA_Knockouts_Tag_Team_Championship" title="TNA Knockouts Tag Team Championship">TNA Knockouts Tag Team Championship</a> (<a href="/wiki/TNA_Knockouts_Tag_Team_Championship#Reigns" title="TNA Knockouts Tag Team Championship">1 time</a>) – with <a href="/wiki/Katarina_Waters" title="Katarina Waters">Winter</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Impact122310Tapings_109-1"><a href="#cite_note-Impact122310Tapings-109">[109]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Impact122310_110-1"><a href="#cite_note-Impact122310-110">[110]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/TNA_Knockout#TNA_Knockouts_Tag_Team_Championship_Tournament_.282010.29" title="TNA Knockout">TNA Knockouts Tag Team Championship Tournament (2010)</a> – with Winter</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/TNA_One_Night_Only#Global_Impact:_USA_vs_The_World" title="TNA One Night Only">Global Impact Tournament (2015)</a> – with Team International <small>(<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Great_Sanada" title="The Great Sanada">The Great Sanada</a>, <a href="/wiki/Drew_Galloway" title="Drew Galloway">Drew Galloway</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magnus_(wrestler)" title="Magnus (wrestler)">Magnus</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Great_Muta" title="The Great Muta">The Great Muta</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tigre_Uno" title="Tigre Uno">Tigre Uno</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bram_(wrestler)" title="Bram (wrestler)">Bram</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rockstar_Spud" title="Rockstar Spud">Rockstar Spud</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mahabali_Shera" title="Mahabali Shera">Khoya</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sonjay_Dutt" title="Sonjay Dutt">Sonjay Dutt</a>)</small></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
